Illinois COVID-19 Vaccine Finder

A tool to help you track down COVID-19 vaccine appointment openings at Illinois pharmacies. Updated every minute.

Step 1: Review your county's availability and IL's eligibility

Be sure to visit your own state's official vaccination website for detailed information about your county's vaccine options and review whether or not you are eligible yet.

You may be able to signup for vaccines with a health providers or there may be other options in your area, in which case you may not need this tool.

Step 2: Use this tool to try and find a pharmacy appointment

If you decide you want to find an appointment at a local pharmacy (and are currently eligible for the vaccine), this tool might be able to help.

Rather than searching around on each pharmacy's website, we'll automatically scan the pharmacy websites and show you any available appointments we can find on one page.

All CVS, Safeway/Albertsons, Sam's Club, Walgreens, and Walmart locations in Illinois are scanned on a regular basis and this page is updated with any available appointments in the state. If you don't see locations near you right now, appointments can come and go quickly so try visiting the page at different times throughout the day.

02/26/2021: Walgreens data is now available in all states! Hopefully it will stay that way ðŸ¤ž. And an improvement for existing Colorado users: Walgreens data should now show first versus second dose appointment information, hopefully making things easier.

Unfortunately, Albertsons/Safeway and Sam's Club remains mostly broken due to changes they've made which block access to this tool, but I'm still trying to improve things. Any feedback is welcome: vaccine@nickm.org or @nickblah. And if you're a coder and have interest in helping out on GitHub, that would be dandy (although the code's still messy)!

About

Finding vaccines seems tough! Hopefully things will become easier soon, but in the meantime, maybe this can help. If you find this useful, feel free to share it around. Get in touch with any questions: vaccine@nickm.org, @nickblah, or GitHub.

I'd like to add additional functionality (scanning additional pharmacies and sending e-mail or text notifications when appointments open up) if this proves useful and as time permits. If you're a computer programmer and would like to contribute, the project is open source on GitHub (it's currently very messy and undocumented, though).
